[10/03/2026, 10:19:25] San Desh: What do Majority (बहुमत) and Two-Thirds Majority (दुई-तिहाइ बहुमत) mean? Let’s understand:

(1) What is a Simple Majority (बहुमत)?
= When a party or coalition has 50% + 1 member of the total MPs, it is called a Simple Majority (बहुमत).

In Nepal’s House of Representatives (प्रतिनिधि सभा):
• Directly elected (प्रत्यक्ष): 165
• Proportional representation (समानुपातिक): 110
• Total MPs (कुल सांसद): 275

• Majority = 138 MPs or more (१३८ जना वा सोभन्दा बढी)

With a Simple Majority (बहुमत), the parliament can:
• Form the government (सरकार गठन)
• Elect the Prime Minister (प्रधानमन्त्री चयन)
• Pass ordinary laws (साधारण कानून पास)
• Approve the national budget (बजेट पारित) etc.

In short: A Simple Majority (बहुमत) is enough to run the government.

(2) What is a Two-Thirds Majority (दुई-तिहाइ बहुमत)?
= When two-thirds (२/३) of the total MPs support something, it is called a Two-Thirds Majority (दुई-तिहाइ बहुमत).

In the House of Representatives (प्रतिनिधि सभा):
275 × 2/3 = 184 MPs

• 184 MPs or more (१८४ जना वा सोभन्दा बढी) is considered a Two-Thirds Majority (दुई-तिहाइ बहुमत).

With a Two-Thirds Majority (दुई-तिहाइ बहुमत), parliament can:
• Amend the Constitution (संविधान संशोधन)
• Make major national decisions like changes in federal structure or provincial boundaries (संघीय संरचना, प्रदेश सिमाना)
• Pass laws that significantly change the balance of power (शक्ति सन्तुलन बदल्ने कानुनी व्यवस्था)
• Impeach high officials such as the President, Vice President, or Chief Justice (राष्ट्रपति, उपराष्ट्रपति, प्रधानन्यायाधीशमाथि महाभियोग) etc.

[23/04/2026, 16:35:17] ~ Nisha: This is a free of cost event for the participants, and you can submit the paper as an individual or as a team of maximum 5 people.
Registration of the team (or individual), and the submission, will all be done online through the Bank’s website. For teams, just one registration per team needs to be done
Papers will be reviewed by the Bank’s Technical Paper Reviewing Committee, and will be classified into three categories:
Extremely Useful
Intutive
Not useful enough
(Sorted as: “Extremely Useful” being the highest rank, and “Not Useful Enough” being the lowest.)

Only the participants whose result belongs to “Extremely Useful”, and “Intuitive” category, will receive the digital shareable certificates via registered email (For teams, all the individual members will get the certificate), and the results will also be made public via the Bank’s Website, and the Social Media Channels. Whereas, the results of “Not Useful Enough” category will be notified to the respective participant(s) through email, but will not be made public.
The participants who secured “Extremely Useful”, and “Intuitive” category will be auto-qualify for the Hackathon event to be held from 29nd May to 31st May, 2026.
There will be multiple winners under several categories on the Hackathon Event, which include Monetary Prizes, and Public Recognition through media platforms.
The deadline to submit the paper is 5:00 P.M.- May 4th, 2026(NST)
Refer to the Challenges Page for the detailed problem statement and the submission format.
Please reach out to us on hackathon@gibl.com.np in case of any inquiry.
